Method: 提出检索增强的小语言模型框架，使用形式概念分析（FCA）作为符号验证循环。从种子属性开始，FCA在增长的形式背景上提出蕴涵；检索增强的SLM预言机验证每个蕴涵并返回反例；预言机还支持incidence判断、一致性检查和属性提议。

Result: 在Orphadata构建的罕见共济失调场景中，检索增强的10种子运行获得关系F1为0.29-0.52，闭包蕴涵F1为0.22-0.30。更大种子集增加了评估蕴涵数量并改善蕴涵F1。消融显示固定对象-属性设置下incidence判断可提升闭包蕴涵得分，但识别正对象-属性对仍然困难。

Conclusion: 该方法通过FCA符号验证与检索增强SLM的结合，实现了可检查的知识扩展过程；蕴涵得分较低反映了派生蕴涵评估的严格性；未来需改进正对象-属性对的识别能力。

Abstract: Ontology construction requires deciding which objects, attributes, and structural relations should be accepted as valid knowledge. Language models can propose such structures from text, but their outputs can still be unsupported or inconsistent. This paper proposes a retrieval-augmented small language model (SLM) framework that uses formal concept analysis (FCA) as a symbolic verification loop for knowledge expansion. Starting from seed attributes, FCA proposes implications over a growing formal context. A retrieval-grounded SLM oracle then validates each implication or returns a counterexample. The oracle also supports incidence judgments, consistency checks, and attribute proposals, making accepted implications, counterexamples, contradictions, and corrections inspectable. In a rare ataxia setting constructed from Orphadata resources, retrieval-grounded 10-seed runs obtain relation F1 of 0.29-0.52 and closure-based implication F1 of 0.22-0.30. Larger seed sets increase the number of evaluated implications and often improve implication F1. The lower implication scores reflect a stricter evaluation of derived implications, where one missed or extra relation can affect several implication judgments. Ablations show that incidence judgments in a fixed object-attribute setting can improve closure-based implication scores. However, identifying positive object-attribute pairs remains difficult even when the candidate objects and attributes are fixed.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散语言模型（DLMs）作为自回归模型的有前景替代方案出现，但与标准扩散方法不同，DLMs并未显式地以时间步为条件。这引出一个自然问题：这些模型是否内部表征了去噪进度，以及这种信息如何在模型下游被利用。

Method: 通过探针（probes）从模型残差流中提取与扩散时间步相关的潜在表征信号；沿与推断时间步相关的低维子空间对模型进行操控（steering），以调节其对去噪进度的感知。

Result: DLMs确实编码了去噪进度的潜在表征，该信号可跨层可靠解码；操控该信号可系统性地改变模型置信度和熵；该表征在激活空间中具有结构化和可解释的几何特性。

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型内部隐式地编码了去噪进度信息，且该信息具有可解释的几何结构，通过操控可实现对模型行为的可预测调节。

Abstract: Diffusion Language Models (DLMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to autoregressive models. Unlike standard diffusion-based approaches, DLMs are not explicitly conditioned on a timestep, raising a natural question: do these models internally represent denoising progress, and how is such information used downstream? In this work, we show that DLMs do in fact encode a latent representation related to the diffusion timestep within their residual streams. We find that this signal can be reliably extracted using probes across layers, indicating that denoising progress is decodable from internal activations. We further demonstrate that steering the model along a low-dimensional subspace associated with the inferred timestep allows us to systematically modulate its notion of denoising progress, leading to predictable changes in model confidence and entropy. Finally, we analyse the geometry of the identified representation, showing that it exhibits structured and interpretable properties in activation space, and shedding light on how such a signal is processed by these models.

### [225] [Safety Testing LLM Agents at Scale: From Risk Discovery to Evidence-Grounded Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01793)
*Yunhao Feng,Ruixiao Lin,Ming Wen,Qinqin He,Yanming Guo,Yifan Ding,Yutao Wu,Jialuo Chen,Yunhao Chen,Xiaohu Du,Jianan Ma,Zixing Chen,Zhuoer Xu,Xingjun Ma,Xinhao Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Vera是一个端到端的自动化安全测试框架，通过文献驱动的风险发现、组合式安全用例生成和自适应执行三阶段流水线，对非确定性LLM智能体进行可扩展、可维护的安全评估。在四个主流智能体框架上测试发现平均攻击成功率达93.9%，并发布了包含1600个可执行安全用例的Vera-Bench基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全测试依赖专家设计的违规场景和硬编码规则评估，随着智能体系统快速演进，扩展成本高昂，缺乏可自动化、可维护的安全测试方法。

Method: 提出Vera框架，包含三阶段自增强流水线：(1) 文献驱动的风险发现，持续发现和结构化新兴风险；(2) 跨风险维度组合生成可执行安全用例，包含具体安全目标、程序化初始状态和确定性验证谓词；(3) 自适应执行，在隔离沙箱中运行异构智能体，通过控制智能体引导多轮交互，并基于环境状态和工具调用证据进行可验证的判定。

Result: 在OpenClaw、Hermes、Codex、Claude Code四个生产级智能体框架上评估，多通道攻击平均成功率93.9%；发布Vera-Bench包含1600个可执行安全用例，覆盖124个风险类别和三种执行环境。

Conclusion: 模块化、可执行的安全测试基础设施对于大规模、严格且可维护地评估快速演进的智能体系统至关重要。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly perform autonomous actions through external tools, leading to complex and evolving safety risks. However, existing safety testing targets expert-designed safety violations, and the corresponding outcomes are evaluated by hard-coded rules, making them costly to extend as agents evolve. To this end, we present Vera, an end-to-end automated safety testing framework that instantiates software engineering testing principles for non-deterministic agents through a three-stage, self-reinforcing pipeline. First, a literature-driven exploration continuously discovers and structures emerging risks into taxonomies of safety risks, attack methods, and tool execution environments. Second, combinatorial composition across taxonomy dimensions produces executable safety cases, each specifying a concrete safety goal, a programmatically constructed initial state, and a deterministic verification predicate grounded in observable artifacts. Third, adaptive execution runs heterogeneous agents in isolated sandboxes where a control agent steers multi-turn interaction based on runtime observations, while evidence-grounded verifiers judge outcomes from environment state and tool-call evidence rather than model self-report. We evaluate Vera on four production agent frameworks (OpenClaw, Hermes, Codex, Claude Code), revealing substantial safety weaknesses, with average attack success rates reaching 93.9\% under multi-channel attacks; we also release Vera-Bench, comprising 1600 executable safety cases spanning 124 risk categories across three execution settings. These results indicate that modular, executable testing infrastructure is essential for rigorous and maintainable safety evaluation of rapidly evolving agentic systems at scale. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/Yunhao-Feng/Vera.

### [229] [CLAP: Closed-Loop Training, Evaluation, and Release Control for Domain Agent Post-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01846)
*Fangfei Li,Chenyang Zhao,Long Wang,Feng Tian,Zhiyue Zheng,Lv Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CLAP提出了一种闭环智能体后训练方法，通过数据验证、目标/证据归一化、奖励/KL诊断、离线门控和应用链回放，系统性地管理业务数据到适配器发布的流程。在五个制造场景批次上，LoRA-SFT平均提升微弱（总分+0.0098，通过率+0.0240，证据准确率+0.0280），但仅3/5批次改善，GRPO暴露出高KL风险，应用链回放显示RAG对事实提取至关重要。结论支持采用集成数据-训练-评估-发布的闭环管理，而非依赖训练完成或单一离线分数。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域智能体面临业务数据噪声大、后训练收益不确定、离线/应用失配以及适配器发布风险等问题，现有方法缺乏系统性的端到端管理机制。

Method: CLAP方法将业务数据转化为结构化SFT样本、决策偏好样本、留出集、风险诊断和发布门控记录，集成了数据验证、目标/证据归一化、奖励/KL诊断、离线门控和应用链回放五大环节。

Abstract: Domain agents often face noisy business data, uncertain post-training gains, offline/application mismatch, and adapter-release risk. This paper presents CLAP (Closed-Loop Agent Post-training), a closed-loop method that converts business data into structured SFT samples, decision-preference samples, holdout sets, risk diagnostics, and release-gate records. CLAP combines data validation, target/evidence normalization, reward/KL diagnosis, offline gates, and application-chain replay to decide whether an adapter is suitable for the target application chain. On five anonymized manufacturing-scenario batches, QLoRA-style LoRA-SFT yields modest average gains: overall score increases by 0.0098, pass rate by 0.0240, and evidence accuracy by 0.0280, while hallucination and wrong facts decrease. Yet only 3 of 5 batches improve, some batches regress, and GRPO exposes high KL risks. Application-chain replay further shows that RAG is necessary for factual extraction; under the same 3B backbone and 100 replay cases, an application-RAG-oriented LoRA-SFT adapter improves value, core fields, and answer-evidence doc/page matching over base+RAG, but increases latency. These results support managing domain-agent post-training through an integrated data-training-evaluation-release loop rather than relying on training completion or a single offline score.

### [230] [Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01859)
*Joshua Adrian Cahyono*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出STEER攻击方法，通过将触发拒绝的关键词翻译为低资源语言，绕过LLM安全机制，在多个8B模型上达到93-96.7%攻击成功率，并跨模型迁移至GPT-4o-mini，揭示了英语主导的安全训练在多语言输入下的泛化漏洞。

Motivation: LLM安全训练主要以英语进行，其在低资源语言和代码混合场景下的泛化能力未知，存在安全机制失效的知识漏洞。

Method: 提出STEER攻击：利用梯度引导识别对拒绝行为贡献最大的关键词，迭代将其翻译为低资源语言以抑制拒绝响应，同时保留有害意图。

Result: 在六个8B开源模型上，STEER在JailbreakBench达93.0%攻击成功率，在AdvBench达96.7%，优于随机代码混合和GCG；攻击提示可迁移至GPT-4o-mini，达35.5%成功率。

Conclusion: 以英语为主的安全对齐不能假定在多语言输入上通用，需要更广泛的语言覆盖和对分布外输入的检测与拒答机制。

Abstract: Safety training for large language models (LLMs) is conducted predominantly in English, leaving uncertain how well safety mechanisms generalize to low-resource languages and mixed-language code-switching. We show that this creates an epistemic gap in which models confidently generate harmful responses for inputs that fall outside the distribution of their safety training. To study this phenomenon, we introduce STEER (Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement), a gradient-guided attack that identifies words contributing most strongly to the model's refusal behavior and iteratively translates them into low-resource languages to suppress refusal while preserving harmful intent. Across six open-source 8B-parameter models, STEER achieves attack success rates of up to 93.0% on JailbreakBench and 96.7% on AdvBench, outperforming random code-switching and Greedy Coordinate Gradient (GCG). The resulting prompts also transfer to GPT-4o-mini, achieving a 35.5% attack success rate without requiring access to the target model, suggesting that the underlying weakness is not specific to a single architecture. These findings demonstrate that safety mechanisms aligned primarily on English cannot be assumed to generalize across multilingual inputs. We argue that improving multilingual safety requires broader coverage during alignment and mechanisms that explicitly detect and abstain on out-of-distribution inputs.

</details>

*Dawei Ren,Yan Zhang,Hongying Tang,Qiaoling Zhou,Jianpo Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CamoNAS提出了一种频率感知的多分辨率神经架构搜索框架，自动搜索细胞级操作和网络级下采样路径，并结合RGB频率双流架构（可学习小波变换），在四个COD基准数据集上达到最先进性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统COD模型依赖手工设计的架构和多尺度特征融合，这些设计往往基于直觉而非系统搜索，缺乏对伪装目标弱边缘和模糊边界的针对性优化。

Method: 提出CamoNAS框架，包含：(1) 层次化搜索空间，同时搜索细胞级操作和网络级下采样路径；(2) RGB频率双流架构，其中可学习小波变换作为频率流补充RGB空间流。

Abstract: Camouflaged Object Detection (COD) aims to locate and segment objects that blend into their surroundings, presenting challenges due to weak edge cues and ill-defined boundaries. Traditional COD models rely on hand-designed architectures and multi-scale feature fusion, which are often guided by intuition rather than systematic search. This paper introduces CamoNAS, a frequency-aware multi-resolution Neural Architecture Search (NAS) framework for COD. CamoNAS automatically searches both cell-level operations and network-level downsampling paths, forming a hierarchical search space tailored to detect camouflaged objects. Additionally, it adopts an RGB frequency dual-stream architecture, where a learnable wavelet transform complements the RGB spatial stream. CamoNAS achieves state-of-the-art performance on four COD benchmarks (CAMO, COD10K, NC4K, CHAMELEON), highlighting the effectiveness of NAS for COD. Our code is available at https://github.com/rendaweiSIMIT/CamoNAS.

### [232] [SkillCoach: Self-Evolving Rubrics for Evaluating and Enhancing Agentic Skill-Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01874)
*Jiayin Zhu,Kelong Mao,Yudong Guo,Dengbo He,Sulong Xu,Simiu Gu,Yutao Yue*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillCoach是一个自我演进的评估框架，通过从真实轨迹中推导技能导向的过程评估标准，从技能选择、遵循、组合和反思四个维度评估LLM智能体的技能使用质量，并将过程质量与最终任务成功区分开来，从而改进评估和训练监督信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中，最终验证器的成功信号过于粗糙，无法可靠地评估和训练智能体的技能使用能力，因为智能体可能通过试错、选择干扰技能、跳过必要步骤、错误组合工作流或遗漏最终检查等方式偶然成功。

Method: SkillCoach从真实轨迹中推导技能导向的过程评估标准（rubrics），从四个维度（技能选择、技能遵循、技能组合、技能导向的反思）评估轨迹，并将外部验证器作为独立的结果信号，使过程质量与偶然任务成功得以区分。演进后的评估标准进一步作为过程监督信号用于筛选高质量训练轨迹。

Result: 实验表明，演进后的评估标准显著提升了评估质量，能够揭示被最终准确率掩盖的失败，并提供比仅基于结果过滤更强的监督信号来增强智能体的技能使用能力。

Conclusion: SkillCoach通过细粒度的过程评估框架有效区分了过程质量与偶然成功，为智能体的技能使用评估和训练提供了更可靠的监督信号。

Abstract: Skills are becoming a reusable operational layer for LLM agents, encoding SOPs, domain rules, tool workflows, scripts, and validation routines. In realistic skill repositories, overlapping skills make reliable skill-use difficult. Final verifier success is too coarse for both evaluation and training, since an agent may pass through trial and error while selecting distractor skills, skipping required steps, composing workflows incorrectly or omitting final checks. We introduce SkillCoach, a self-evolving rubric framework for evaluating and enhancing agentic skill-use. SkillCoach derives skill-grounded process rubrics from real rollouts and evaluates trajectories along four dimensions: skill selection, skill following, skill composition, and skill-grounded reflection. It keeps the external verifier as a separate outcome signal, allowing process quality to be distinguished from accidental task success. The evolved rubrics further serve as process supervision for selecting high-quality training trajectories. Experiments show that evolved rubrics substantially improve evaluation quality, expose failures hidden by final accuracy, and provide stronger supervision signals than outcome-only filtering for enhancing agentic skill-use.

### [233] [Spec-AUF: Accept-Until-Fail Training under Train-Inference Misalignment for Masked Block Drafters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01893)
*Tianjian Yang,Meng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AUF（Acceptance-Unaware Fix）方法，通过截断条件交叉熵的支持范围（仅保留到第一个预测失败的token），使块级草稿模型的训练损失聚焦于推理时实际会被接受的前缀。在Qwen3-8B上，AUF将DFlash的平均接受长度从2.40提升至2.61，且在各基准上均有增益，并迁移至Domino架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准块级草稿模型使用全块交叉熵损失训练，对每个位置都监督其预测与黄金续写的匹配，但推理时从左到右验证，第一个被拒绝的token之后的所有预测都会被丢弃。这种训练-推理不匹配导致训练资源浪费在推理时无用的位置上。

Method: AUF在损失层面将交叉熵的支持范围截断至草稿模型第一次预测失败的位置之前（即仅保留被接受的前缀），无需辅助目标、验证器rollout或修改推理流程。对于缺乏输入侧黄金前缀条件通道的掩码块草稿器，AUF通过在损失侧近似前缀敏感监督来实现。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B上，AUF将DFlash的平均发射长度τ从2.40提升至2.61（六个基准均正向）。迁移至Domino双分支头从2.56提升至2.68。此外，仅使用衰减基线虽在共享块掩码上达到更高token准确率，但解码效果更差；在DFlash上，一旦AUF截断支持范围，标准指数位置衰减权重变得经验上无效。

Conclusion: AUF通过简单的损失支持截断有效缓解了块级草稿模型的训练-推理不匹配问题，提升了推测解码效率，且说明位置衰减权重在AUF下是冗余的。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates autoregressive generation by drafting a block of tokens that the target model verifies left-to-right, committing only the longest accepted prefix. Block (DLM-style) drafters predict the whole block in parallel, which is fast but trained with a full-block cross-entropy that supervises every position against the gold continuation -- even though inference discards every token after the first rejection. Recent acceptance-aware objectives patch this by reweighting the full-block loss; we instead use teacher-forced learning as a motivation for how supervision should concentrate on the accepted prefix. A mask-only block drafter has no input-side channel for gold-prefix conditioning, so AUF approximates that prefix-sensitive supervision on the loss side by keeping the cross-entropy support only through the drafter's first predicted failure. AUF is a single, detached change to the CE support -- no auxiliary objective, no verifier rollouts, and no change to the inference pipeline or the exactness contract. Within fixed drafter backbones and serving settings on Qwen3-8B, AUF raises the DFlash drafter's average emitted length $τ$, averaged over six benchmarks, from 2.40 to 2.61, with a gain on every benchmark, and transfers to Domino's two-branch head (2.56 to 2.68). Two findings sharpen the picture: the decay-only baseline reaches higher token accuracy on the shared block mask yet decodes worse, and on DFlash, once AUF truncates the support, the standard exponential position-decay weighting becomes empirically inert.

### [234] [Rethinking Complexity Metrics for LLM-Integrated Applications: Beyond Source Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01903)
*Zihao Xu,Yuekang Li,Gelei Deng,Yi Liu,Zhenchang Xing*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HECATE是首个同时评估LLM应用提示层和代码层复杂度的工具。基于Prompt-as-Specification形式化方法和25个复杂度维度，生成52个候选指标，经118个组件验证后仅10个指标显著有效，其中提示层指标（结构性广度）为复杂度评估提供了独立于代码层的新维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有复杂度指标仅作用于代码层面，无法捕捉LLM集成应用中提示层的行为逻辑，而这类应用的运行时行为主要源自提示层而非代码本身。

Method: 提出HECATE工具，核心包括：1) Prompt-as-Specification形式化方法（基于Hoare逻辑）；2) 从已发表分类学中提取25个复杂度维度，生成52个候选指标；3) 从18个开源仓库收集118个组件，以版本历史维护活动作为复杂度代理进行实证验证；4) 使用统计方法剔除受代码规模影响的指标。

Result: 仅10个指标通过统计检验：7个为新提出的结构广度指标（如LLM调用点、记忆属性、提示模板等），3个为传统指标（RFC具有广度特征，Halstead N和V仅作为规模残余效应存在）；提示层指标在加入最强代码层协变量后仍保持显著性；在6个保留仓库的20个组件上，两个最佳指标仍能预测维护工作量。

Conclusion: 提示复杂度是独立于代码复杂度的新维度，结构广度（而非单纯体量）是衡量LLM应用复杂度的有效方式；HECATE的指标具有良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: LLM-integrated applications blend natural language prompts with program code, and much of their runtime behavior originates in the prompt layer rather than in the code itself. Existing complexity metrics, however, operate solely at the code level and therefore overlook this behavioral logic entirely. We present HECATE, the first tool designed to assess complexity in both the prompt and code layers of such applications. Central to HECATE is Prompt-as-Specification, a Hoare-logic-inspired formalism that interprets every prompt as a specification of intended behavior. Grounded in 25 complexity dimensions identified across published taxonomies, the tool generates 52 candidate metrics. We assess each metric against 118 components collected from 18 open-source repositories, relying on maintenance activity derived from version history as an empirical proxy for complexity, and discard any metric that loses significance once code size is accounted for. Only ten metrics withstand this test. Seven belong to our newly introduced set; rather than measuring sheer volume, each tallies structurally distinct elements, such as LLM call sites, memory attributes, and prompt templates, an attribute we call structural breadth. Of the three surviving conventional metrics, RFC exhibits a similar breadth-oriented character, while Halstead N and V survive only as a residual effect of size; our top-performing metrics exceed all three. Crucially, the prompt-layer metrics retain significance even when the strongest code-level metric is added as a covariate, establishing prompt complexity as a dimension in its own right. A final validation on 20 components spanning six held-out repositories shows that the two best-performing metrics continue to predict maintenance effort, supporting their generalizability beyond the training set.

</details>

*Chiwang Luk,Matin Mohammad Najafi,Zhifeng Jia,Wei Yang,Xiuchang Li,Jinwei Zhu,Yang Ren,Lei Chen,Gao Cong*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ContextSniper实现Sniper功能：检索候选代码和运行时证据，通过混合检索信号排序，利用意图感知上下文门过滤长输出，返回紧凑证据包，同时将可恢复的源上下文保留在提示之外。

Result: 在SWE-bench Lite上，OpenClaw总token减少51.5%，成本降低36.4%，提交修复率从26.0%降至24.0%；Claude Code总token减少38.9%，成本降低27.3%，提交修复率从32.0%降至30.0%。

Conclusion: ContextSniper在仅轻微降低修复率的前提下，显著减少了token消耗和成本，证明了精确证据选择策略在仓库级程序修复中的有效性。

Abstract: Large language model agents can repair real repository issues, but they often spend large context budgets on whole-file reads, broad searches, and long terminal outputs where useful evidence is mixed with irrelevant code and logs. This paper presents ContextSniper, AntTrail's token-efficient code memory layer for repository-level program repair. As the coding specialization of AntTrail's broader agent memory engine, ContextSniper implements the Sniper feature for precision evidence selection: it retrieves candidate code and runtime evidence, ranks it with hybrid retrieval signals, filters long outputs through an intention-aware context gate, and returns compact evidence packets while preserving recoverable source context outside the prompt. We evaluate ContextSniper on SWE-bench Lite with OpenClaw and Claude Code, using 50 task runs per host-agent condition. ContextSniper reduces total token use by 51.5% and logged cost by 36.4% for OpenClaw, and reduces total token use by 38.9% and estimated cost by 27.3% for Claude Code. Submitted-resolution rates decrease slightly, from 26.0% to 24.0% for OpenClaw and from 32.0% to 30.0% for Claude Code. ContextSniper's pilot testing scripts are open-sourced at https://github.com/Calluking/ContextSniper

### [236] [ElephantAgent: Contextual State Continuity in Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01919)
*Jiankai Jin,Xiangzheng Zhang,Zhao Liu,Wenzhuo Xu,Dongdong Yang,Deyue Zhang,Quanchen Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ElephantAgent是一种通过强制执行上下文状态连续性来防御上下文状态投毒攻击的协议，它利用复制可信硬件维护可线性化的授权状态转换账本，并结合历史可追溯性实现事后审计和状态恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agent系统通过调用外部工具和维护持久内存来增强能力，但这些外部依赖引入了新的攻击面。现有的工具和内存投毒攻击表明，恶意构造的工具描述和投毒内存可以隐蔽地偏置Agent行为，其根源在于Agent规划和执行的上下文状态缺乏可验证的连续性。

Method: 定义上下文状态为Agent整个上下文中有限的安全关键子集（如工具状态和内存）；在处理每个查询前重新计算本地上下文状态的摘要并与最新授权摘要对比验证；利用复制可信硬件维护可线性化的授权上下文状态转换账本，检测带外状态篡改；针对带内语义滥用，提供历史可追溯性，支持有条件的事后审计和恢复到已知良好的先前状态。

Result: ElephantAgent能够检测带外状态篡改，并通过历史可追溯性机制处理带内语义滥用，实现上下文状态投毒攻击的防御。

Conclusion: 受到Nimble等先前状态连续性机制的启发，ElephantAgent将这种保护扩展到Agent系统不断演化的上下文状态中，有效解决了Agent系统因外部依赖而面临的新安全威胁。

Abstract: Agentic systems enhance their capabilities by invoking external tools and maintaining persistent memory. However, these external dependencies introduce novel attack surfaces. Recent tool and memory poisoning attacks show that maliciously crafted tool descriptors and poisoned memory can covertly bias agent behavior. These threats reflect a deeper issue: the lack of verifiable continuity in the agent's contextual state for planning and execution. We present ElephantAgent, a protocol that enforces Contextual State Continuity to defend against contextual state poisoning. Inspired by prior state-continuity mechanisms (e.g., Nimble), ElephantAgent extends this protection to the evolving contextual state of agentic systems. We define the contextual state as the bounded, security-critical subset of the agent's entire context (e.g., tool state and memory). Before processing each query, ElephantAgent recomputes the digest of the local contextual state and verifies it against the latest authorized digest. Using replicated trusted hardware, ElephantAgent maintains a linearizable ledger of authorized contextual state transitions and detects out-of-band state tampering. To handle in-band semantic abuse, ElephantAgent additionally provides Historical Traceability, enabling conditional post-hoc audit and recovery to a known-good prior state.

### [237] [A-TMA: Decoupling State-Aware Memory Failures in Long-Term Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01935)
*Zitong Shi,Yixuan Tang,Anthony Kum Hoe Tung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对LLM智能体长期记忆中的状态协调失败问题（幻影记忆），提出了ATMA状态感知覆盖层，在银行维护、检索和答案解析三个层面优化，并通过LTP基准测试验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM记忆系统在用户事实发生变化时，旧事实、当前事实和过渡事实会混合存储在记忆库中，导致检索时混淆并误导答案模型，这种状态协调失败称为"幻影记忆"（ghost memory）。

Method: 提出ATMA（状态感知覆盖层），在三个层面优化：1）银行维护层：保留被取代记录和过渡记录；2）检索层：为查询请求的状态视图构建证据包；3）答案解析层：将当前、历史和过渡标签暴露给QA模型。同时构建LTP（LoCoMo Temporal Plus）冲突密集基准用于评估。

Result: 在LTP基准上，Graphiti+ATMA相比Graphiti冲突准确率提升0.240；在LoCoMo上，Graphiti+ATMA将时间F1从0.0295提升至0.1705。

Conclusion: 明确的状态角色划分可以减少被最终QA准确率掩盖的记忆失败，但增益与宿主系统相关。同时呼吁对银行、检索和答案层面的失败进行解耦评估。

Abstract: Long term memory lets LLM agents act as persistent assistants, but user facts change. A useful memory system must know what is true now, what used to be true, and what changed. We study \emph{ghost memory}, a state coordination failure in which old, current, and transition facts coexist in the memory bank, remain mixed during retrieval, and mislead the answer model. We argue that memory systems should be understood and optimized from three levels: bank maintenance, retrieval, and answer time resolution. We propose ATMA, a state aware overlay for existing memory systems. ATMA keeps superseded and transition records in the bank, builds evidence packets for the query's requested state view, and exposes current, historical, and transition labels to QA. We further call for decoupled evaluation of bank, retrieval, and answer level failures, since final QA accuracy can hide where ghost memory occurs. To make this failure measurable, we build LTP (LoCoMo Temporal Plus), a conflict heavy benchmark for ghost memory, and evaluate on LoCoMo for long conversation generalization. On LTP, Graphiti+ATMA improves conflict accuracy by 0.240 absolute over Graphiti. On LoCoMo, Graphiti+ATMA raises temporal F1 from 0.0295 to 0.1705. The gains are host dependent, but they indicate that explicit state roles can reduce memory failures hidden by final QA accuracy.

### [238] [Atomic Task Graph: A Unified Framework for Agentic Planning and Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01942)

Motivation: 现有LLM智能体方法要么依赖更大规模模型（计算成本高），要么依赖任务特定微调（泛化性差）；基于提示的控制虽免训练且通用，但子任务间的输入输出依赖隐含在文本轨迹中，导致已验证的中间结果难以复用。

Method: 提出ATG统一控制框架：规划阶段递归将高层任务分解为子任务，形成有向无环图序列；执行阶段利用暴露的依赖关系实现独立分支并行执行；检测到失败时利用图演化历史定位错误源并仅修复受影响区域。

Result: 在三个交互式基准上，仅使用7B-8B骨干模型，ATG在成功率和执行效率上一致优于强基线。

Conclusion: ATG通过显式图结构有效解决了子任务依赖暴露与中间结果复用问题，在无需大模型或微调的前提下显著提升了多步任务求解的性能和效率。

Abstract: LLM-based agents have shown strong potential for solving complex multi-step tasks, yet existing performance improvements often rely on either scaling to larger backbone models or task-specific fine-tuning. The former incurs substantial computational costs, while the latter typically generalizes poorly across different tasks. Although prompt-based control is training-free and broadly applicable, existing methods still leave input-output dependencies between subtasks implicit in textual trajectories, making verified intermediate results difficult to reuse. To address these limitations, we propose Atomic Task Graph (ATG), a unified control framework for planning and execution. Specifically, ATG maintains an explicit graph to expose dependencies and support reuse. During planning, it recursively decomposes a high-level task into subtasks, forming a sequence of directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) whose evolution can be traced. During execution, the dependencies exposed by ATG allow independent branches to be executed in parallel, thereby improving execution efficiency. When failures are detected, ATG leverages the graph evolution history to localize the error source and repair only the affected region, preserving validated regions unchanged. Experiments show that ATG consistently outperforms strong baselines in success rate and execution efficiency across three interactive benchmarks using only 7B-8B backbones.

</details>

*Hamed Babaei Giglou,Jennifer D'Souza,Andrei Aioanei,Nandana Mihindukulasooriya,Sören Auer*

Conclusion: 有效的本体学习需要通过类似OntoLearner的跨领域、多任务基准测试平台来实现；未来研究方向应聚焦于弥合模型知识编码与本体组织结构之间的结构性鸿沟。

Abstract: Ontology learning (OL) aims to automatically construct structured knowledge models from text, yet progress remains fragmented across methods, domains, and evaluation practices. Despite decades of research, OL lacks a shared infrastructure for systematic evaluation and ontology access. This absence has hindered progress and fragmented research, leaving the central challenges of OL largely unaddressed. We introduce OntoLearner, a modular, cross-domain, and first-of-its-kind framework that unifies ontology access, large language model (LLM)-driven learning pipelines, and standardized benchmarking. OntoLearner releases 180 machine-readable ontologies spanning 22 domains and provides pipeline-ready datasets with train/dev/test splits for three core OL tasks: term typing, taxonomy discovery, and non-taxonomic relation extraction. Using this infrastructure, we conduct a large-scale empirical study of OL, evaluating 22 retrieval models and 12 LLMs across domains and tasks. The results converge on a finding that reframes the central challenge of OL: failure modes scale with ontological complexity rather than model size or architectural sophistication. The primary bottleneck is not model capability, but a structural mismatch between how models encode knowledge and how ontologies organize it. These findings establish that effective OL is reachable through the cross-domain, multi-task benchmarking enabled by OntoLearner. OntoLearner is open-source (MIT license) at https://github.com/sciknoworg/OntoLearner/.

### [240] [Multimodal Knowledge Edit-Scoped Generalization for Online Recursive MLLM Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01978)
*Siyuan Li,Youyuan Zhang,Ruitong Liu,Junxi Wang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ScopeEdit，一种范围感知的在线多模态大模型编辑方法，通过将每次更新分解为模态局部吸收分支和证据门控共享泛化分支，在正交低秩空间中实现范围分离的写入几何，从而控制编辑的传播边界，在保证编辑可靠性的同时提升跨模态迁移与局域性之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线多模态编辑方法主要关注编辑可靠性和长期稳定性，但忽视了编辑的语义边界控制。实验发现实例级编辑成功后，既无法保证向有效跨模态变体迁移，也无法防止向无关输入泄漏，存在"范围鸿沟"问题。

Method: 提出ScopeEdit，包含两个分支：1) 模态局部吸收分支，支持稳定的编辑吸收；2) 证据门控共享泛化分支，仅在视觉和文本证据充分对齐时允许跨模态传播。两分支在正交低秩空间中执行范围分离的写入几何，并通过Sherman-Morrison递归维护分支级预条件子，保持恒定的单次编辑开销。

Result: 在多种基准、长时编辑流、MLLM主干网络、真实世界VLKEB场景以及复杂视觉-语言架构上的实验表明，ScopeEdit持续改善了范围内跨模态迁移与范围外局域性之间的权衡，同时保持了编辑可靠性、稳定性和在线效率。

Conclusion: ScopeEdit通过显式建模编辑的传播边界，将多模态编辑从简单的实例纠正提升为对编辑传播范围的控制，为在线多模态大模型编辑提供了更精细的语义边界管理方案。

Abstract: Online multimodal knowledge editing requires injecting a continual stream of visual-textual corrections into multimodal large language models (MLLMs) with bounded overhead and minimal disruption to unrelated behaviors. Existing editors mainly emphasize edit reliability and long-horizon stability, but rarely control the semantic boundary of each edit. Our pilot analyses of post-edit behaviors and internal neuronal activities reveal a scope gap behind reliable edits: instance-level success neither guarantees transfer to valid cross-modal variants nor prevents leakage to unrelated inputs, while edit-related cross-modal responses concentrate in deeper semantic layers. Therefore, we formulate Edit-Scoped Generalization, reframing online MLLM editing from merely correcting an instance to controlling the propagation boundary of each edit. To this end, we propose ScopeEdit, a scope-aware online editor that decomposes each update into a modality-local absorption branch and an evidence-gated shared generalization branch. The local branch supports stable edit absorption, whereas the shared branch enables cross-modal propagation only when visual and textual evidence are sufficiently aligned. Both branches perform scope-separated write geometries in orthogonal low-rank spaces and maintain branch-wise preconditioners via Sherman--Morrison recursions, yielding constant per-edit overhead. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks, long-horizon edit streams, MLLM backbones, real-world VLKEB scenarios, and complex vision-language architectures show that ScopeEdit consistently improves the trade-off between in-scope cross-modal transfer and out-of-scope locality, while preserving edit reliability, stability and online efficiency. Our code is available at https://github.com/lab-klc/ScopeEdit.

### [241] [Episodic-to-Semantic Consolidation Without Identity Drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01988)
*Xue Qin,Simin Luan,Cong Yang,Zhijun Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于确定性函数将情节记忆压缩为语义记忆的知识整合方法，使得自主智能体在更新知识的同时保持加密身份不变，并通过实验验证了该方法的有效性，平均减少了79.82%的无意义规划尝试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期运行的自主智能体面临知识整合与信息完整性之间的结构性矛盾：传统的知识整合方式（如微调模型、重写提示、蒸馏策略、追加反思等）会改变智能体自身，这在受监管的自主部署中是不可接受的，因为智能体受限于针对特定加密认证身份的承诺和审计合约。

Method: 将知识整合视为一个确定性函数 f: M^ep -> M^sem，作用于情节记忆并输出一个独立可寻址的语义知识层；身份哈希不读取 M^sem，因此知识更新不改变智能体的认证身份。给出了智能体表示的形式化描述，通过身份清单哈希输入集的结构引理证明了身份不变性，指定了确定性聚合算法，其输出为具有显式置信度和支持事件来源的可审计数据库行。

Result: 通过合成实验验证了逐字段正确性、跨整合轮次的字节级身份一致性和平均79.82%的无意义规划尝试减少（95% BCa CI [78.02%, 81.49%]，10个种子），与校准的贝叶斯收缩基线对比。

Conclusion: 该构造为自主智能体提供了一种知识更新规范，使智能体通过学习累积可查询事实，同时在其整个运行生命周期中保持加密认证身份的字节级不变性。以具身服务智能体作为运行案例研究。

Abstract: Long-running adaptive intelligent agents face a structural tension between knowledge consolidation and information integrity. Memory consolidation is conventionally treated as an agent-changing operation: a model is fine-tuned, a prompt rewritten, a policy distilled, or a reflection appended to the context that governs future behaviour. In regulated autonomic deployment this is a liability because the agent operates under commitments and audit contracts that bind to a specific, cryptographically certified identity. We propose to treat consolidation not as a mutation of the planner or the identity manifest, but as a deterministic function f: M^ep -> M^sem over episodic memory whose output is a separately addressable semantic knowledge layer; the identity hash does not read M^sem, so consolidation updates knowledge without changing the agent's certified identity. We give a formal account of the agent representation, prove identity invariance through a structural lemma on the manifest's hash-input set, specify a deterministic aggregation algorithm whose outputs are auditable database rows with explicit confidence and supporting-event provenance, and validate the construction with synthetic experiments demonstrating per-field correctness, byte-equal identity across consolidation passes, and a mean 79.82% reduction in unproductive planner attempts (95% BCa CI [78.02%, 81.49%] across 10 seeds) against a calibrated Bayesian-shrunk baseline. The construction is a knowledge-update discipline for autonomic agents in which lessons accumulate as queryable facts while the agent's certified identity remains byte-equal across its operational lifetime, with an embodied service agent as the running case study.

### [243] [InduceKV: Fixed-Footprint Continual Adaptation of Multimodal LLMs via Inducing KV Memories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02010)
*Qianyu Chen,Ziteng Feng,Canran Xiao,Runxuan Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出InduceKV方法，通过双层选择构建紧凑的诱导集，将选定的训练前缀存储为注意力就绪的记忆条目（包含冻结检索键和紧凑的逐层KV负载），在固定内存预算下实现免更新主干模型的持续适应。在多种持续学习场景中，该方法优于PEFT、MoE、回放和提示检索等基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型需要在部署资源受限（固定内存预算）的情况下持续适应新任务和领域，但传统方法（如重复参数更新或不断扩大的回放存储）会随时间累积适应状态，导致内存开销持续增长，无法满足固定足迹部署的需求。

Method: 提出InduceKV，一种基于检索的方法。核心是构建紧凑诱导集：每个条目包含冻结的检索键和紧凑的逐层KV负载，可直接附加到模型的自注意力缓存中。通过双层选择（bilevel selection）实现：轻量级校准拟合检索，同时所选内存平衡当前任务似然、基于锚点的保留性和冻结检索空间中的覆盖度。

Result: 在任务增量指令微调、持续VQA、领域增量适应和终身多模态指令微调等多个场景中，InduceKV在匹配内存预算下持续优于PEFT、MoE、回放和提示检索基线。额外诊断实验表明性能提升并非来自更强的骨干网络、单纯的回放或无限的候选池。

Conclusion: InduceKV通过外部化任务特定更新并以固定内存预算存储紧凑的KV记忆条目，有效解决了多模态大语言模型在部署资源受限下的持续适应问题，为固定足迹持续适应提供了新的有效范式。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models must adapt to evolving tasks and domains, yet continual improvement under bounded deployment footprint remains difficult because repeated parameter updates or growing replay stores can accumulate adaptation state over time. We study fixed-footprint continual adaptation: the deployed adaptation state is kept under a fixed memory budget, while the backbone model is left unchanged and task-specific updates are externalized. We propose InduceKV, a retrieval-based method that stores each selected training prefix as an attention-ready memory entry, consisting of a frozen retrieval key and compact layerwise key--value (KV) payloads that can be appended to the model's self-attention cache. Under a strict memory budget, InduceKV constructs a compact inducing set through bilevel selection: a lightweight calibration is fit for retrieval, while the selected memory balances current-task likelihood, anchor-based retention, and coverage in the frozen retrieval space. Across task-incremental instruction tuning, continual VQA, domain-incremental adaptation, and lifelong multimodal instruction tuning, InduceKV consistently improves over PEFT, MoE, replay, and prompt-retrieval baselines under matched memory budgets. We further report backbone-matched, stage-1 CoIN, compute-matched, and scalability diagnostics, showing that the gains are not due to a stronger backbone, replay alone, or an unbounded candidate pool.

### [244] [Hidden Forgetting in Continual Multimodal Learning: When Accuracy Survives but Grounding Fails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02020)
*Qianyu Chen,Canran Xiao,Runxuan Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的持续学习失败模式——隐藏证据使用遗忘，即在多模态大语言模型持续适应新任务时，答案准确率保持不变，但模型使用的证据通道（视觉、文本、OCR等）发生静默偏移。为解决该问题，提出了RCL框架，通过冻结旧模型作为行为参考，利用反事实通道干预估计证据依赖轮廓，在不增加推理成本的情况下联合优化任务学习、预测保持和依赖保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持续学习指标主要衡量答案是否正确，忽略了多模态模型中证据使用稳定性的评估。作者发现存在一种被忽视的失败模式：模型答案准确率保持不变，但所依赖的证据通道（如视觉、文本、OCR、图表、文档）发生了静默偏移，即“隐藏证据使用遗忘”。

Method: 提出RCL（Reliance-Constrained Continual Learning）框架：1）冻结旧检查点作为行为参考；2）通过反事实通道干预估计教师模型和学生模型的证据依赖轮廓；3）联合优化任务学习、预测保持和证据依赖保持。该方法无需回放数据，不增加推理成本。

Result: 在CoIN、COAST、MCITlib以及一个证据敏感的多模态流上，RCL在最终性能和遗忘减少方面一致优于无回放、PEFT、路由和记忆辅助基线，同时显著降低了模态依赖漂移、主导证据翻转和隐藏遗忘率。

Conclusion: 鲁棒的持续多模态学习不仅需要保持正确答案本身，更需要保持答案背后的证据路径。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models must continually adapt to evolving tasks and domains, yet standard continual learning metrics mainly measure whether old answers remain correct, leaving the stability of multimodal grounding largely unexamined. We study this overlooked failure mode and ask whether a continually adapted MLLM can preserve not only what it answers, but also how it uses visual, textual, OCR, chart, and document evidence. We identify \emph{hidden evidence-use forgetting}, where answer accuracy is retained while the model silently shifts toward different or less grounded evidence channels, and propose \textsc{RCL}, a replay-free reliance-constrained continual learning framework. \textsc{RCL} freezes the previous checkpoint as a behavioral reference, estimates teacher and student evidence-reliance profiles through counterfactual channel interventions, and jointly optimizes task learning, prediction preservation, and reliance preservation without adding inference-time cost. Across CoIN, COAST, MCITlib, and an evidence-sensitive multimodal stream, \textsc{RCL} consistently improves final performance and reduces forgetting over replay-free, PEFT, routing, and memory-assisted baselines, while substantially lowering modality reliance drift, dominant evidence flips, and hidden forgetting rates. These results suggest that robust continual multimodal learning requires preserving the evidence path behind correct answers, not merely the answers themselves.

### [245] [PACE: A Proxy for Agentic Capability Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02032)
*Yueqi Song,Lintang Sutawika,Jiarui Liu,Lindia Tjuatja,Jiayi Geng,Yunze Xiao,Daniel Lee,Aditya Bharat Soni,Vincent Lo,Xiang Yue,Graham Neubig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PACE框架，通过从非智能体基准测试中选取少量原子评估实例构建代理基准，以极低成本（<1%）高精度（MAE<4%, Spearman>0.80）预测智能体基准测试性能，支持模型开发、选择和路由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体基准测试（如SWE-Bench、GAIA）评估成本高昂（数千美元、耗时数天），而非智能体基准测试快速廉价。本文旨在探索能否利用非智能体基准测试中精心挑选的少量原子评估实例，准确预测模型在智能体基准上的性能，从而降低评估开销。

Method: 提出PACE框架：从涵盖原子能力的候选实例池中，通过目标相关性局部选择（target-relevance local selection）和全局信息性选择（globally informative global selection）两种互补策略筛选紧凑子集，然后拟合回归模型将子集得分映射到目标智能体基准得分。由此构建的代理基准称为PACE-Bench。

Result: 在14个模型、4个智能体基准、19个非智能体基准上实验：PACE-Bench预测的LOOCV MAE低于4%，Spearman相关系数高于0.80，成对模型排序准确率约85%，成本仅为完整智能体评估的不到1%。

Conclusion: PACE使从业者能在模型开发、选择和路由过程中以极低开销获得可靠的智能体性能估计，无需完整智能体评估。同时，对所选代理实例的分析揭示了各智能体基准独特需求的能力。

Abstract: Evaluating LLM agents on benchmarks like SWE-Bench and GAIA can be expensive, time-consuming, and requires complex infrastructure. A single evaluation can cost thousands of dollars and take days to complete. In contrast, non-agentic LLM benchmarks that test individual capabilities (e.g., reasoning, code generation) are fast and cheap to run. In this paper, we investigate whether performance on expensive agentic benchmarks can be accurately predicted by the performance on a small, carefully selected subset of atomic evaluation instances. We introduce PACE, a framework that constructs proxy benchmarks by selecting instances from existing non-agentic evaluations whose aggregate scores most reliably predict model performances on agentic benchmarks. Given a pool of candidate instances spanning atomic capabilities, PACE fits a regression that maps a model's scores on a compact subset of source instances to its score on the target agentic benchmark. The subset itself is curated by combining two complementary instance-selection strategies, target-relevance local selection and globally informative global selection. We apply PACE to the 4 target agentic benchmarks in this paper, which yields PACE-Bench, the concrete proxy benchmark that we evaluate in the paper. Experiments across 14 models, 4 agentic benchmarks, and 19 non-agentic benchmarks show that PACE-Bench predicts agentic scores with leave-one-out cross-validation (LOOCV) mean absolute error (MAE) under 4%, Spearman correlation above 0.80, and pairwise model-ranking accuracy around 85%, all at much less than 1% of the full agentic evaluation cost. We further analyze the selected proxy instances, revealing which skills each agentic benchmark uniquely demands. PACE enables practitioners to obtain reliable estimates of agentic performance during model development, selection, and routing, without the overhead of full agent evaluation.

</details>


### [246] [Algebraic Model Counting for Global Analysis of Optimal Decision Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02069)
*Hiroki Arimura*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可解释AI中模型可靠性要求对假设空间进行全局评估，而现有方法缺乏对最优及近优决策树进行穷举分析的统一形式化框架。

Method: 借鉴知识表示中的代数模型计数（AMC），将多种分析任务统一为半环R上的和-积计算；设计动态规划算法实现O*(n^{O(Δ)})时间复杂度；提出模型行为张量，通过张量半环上的卷积积聚合半环值，以处理包含多个树度量的复杂约束。

Result: 算法在特征数n上达到O*(n^{O(Δ)})时间复杂度（隐藏多项式因子），有效解决了决策树假设空间双指数级增长的挑战；通过emtrees软件在真实数据集上验证了框架的有效性。

Conclusion: ADTC提供了一种代数化的全局分析方案，能够构建刻画准确率、大小、公平性等指标间权衡关系的模型画像，支持敏感领域中基于证据的模型选择。

Abstract: Ensuring model reliability in Explainable AI requires a global assessment of the hypothesis space. We propose a formal framework for the exhaustive analysis of optimal and near-optimal decision trees, called Algebraic Decision Tree Counting (ADTC). Inspired by Algebraic Model Counting (AMC) in knowledge representation, ADTC reformulates diverse analytical tasks, such as optimization, counting, and sampling, into a unified sum-of-products computation over a semiring $R$. While the hypothesis space of decision trees is doubly exponential with respect to the maximum depth $Δ$, our dynamic programming algorithm achieves $O^*(n^{O(Δ)})$ time complexity in the number of features $n$, where $O^*$ suppresses polynomial factors. To handle complex constraints consisting of multiple tree metrics, we introduce model behavior tensors that aggregate semiring values via convolution products over a tensor semiring. This algebraic approach efficiently constructs a model profile that captures the global landscape and trade-offs between criteria such as accuracy, size, and fairness. We demonstrate the utility of our software, emtrees, on real-world datasets, illustrating how ADTC facilitates evidence-based model selection in sensitive domains.

<details>

Method: Maven定义了一个以答案为条件的证据状态价值函数，对添加、链接、删除三种证据操作分别设计边际增益、后悔贡献、证据协同和支持度提升等细粒度奖励，并通过GRPO将这些奖励分配到对应的动作跨度上。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning requires models to locate, revise, and synthesize evidence distributed across lengthy inputs. Existing long-context RL methods usually reward final answers or static evidence extraction, offering little feedback on how intermediate actions change the model's evidence state. We propose Maven, a reinforcement learning framework with an editable evidence memory. Maven defines an answer-conditioned evidence-state value and rewards action-level state transitions: add actions are credited by marginal gain and hindsight contribution, link actions by evidence synergy, and drop actions by improved answer support after removing misleading evidence. These rewards are assigned to the corresponding action spans in GRPO. Across Llama and Qwen models on LongBench v2, LongReason, and RULER, Maven outperforms outcome-only RL and evidence-identification baselines, producing more sufficient evidence sets and lower distractor retention. Our results show that long-context RL benefits from optimizing stateful evidence navigation rather than one-shot evidence extraction.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有HSSM依赖固定长度分块或基于相似性的边界检测，这些方法往往与数据的固有时间结构错位。作者主张分块应由预测错误驱动，因为预测错误更直接指示何时需要更长范围的上下文信息。

Method: 提出SUNTA（Surprise-based Nested Temporal Abstraction）：采用解耦训练策略保留惊奇信号；在开放循环预测中，利用内部不一致性作为自上而下的惊奇度量，在想象推演中确定分块边界。

Result: 在2D和3D环境视频预测任务中，SUNTA显著优于基线方法，在250时间步内保持准确预测，而所有基线方法在10步内即退化。

Conclusion: 基于预测错误的惊奇驱动分块策略能更有效地捕捉数据的时空结构，解耦训练策略有效避免了层级坍塌，使HSSM在长时域预测中保持鲁棒性。

Abstract: Hierarchical state-space models (HSSMs) offer a promising approach to long-horizon prediction by segmenting sequences into temporal chunks. However, their performance hinges on how chunk boundaries are determined. While prior HSSMs typically rely on fixed-length chunking or similarity-based boundary detection, these methods often misalign with the intrinsic temporal structure of the data. We argue that chunking should instead be driven by prediction errors, which more directly indicate when longer-range context becomes necessary. Nevertheless, integrating surprise-based chunking into HSSMs introduces critical challenges, including hierarchical collapse during end-to-end training and the absence of surprise signals during open-loop prediction. To address these issues, we propose Surprise-based Nested Temporal Abstraction (SUNTA), a method that employs a decoupled training strategy to preserve surprise signals and uses internal inconsistency as a top-down surprise metric to determine chunk boundaries within imagined rollouts. Experiments on video prediction tasks in 2D and 3D environments demonstrate that SUNTA outperforms baselines, uniquely maintaining accurate predictions over 250 timesteps, whereas all baselines degrade within the first 10 timesteps.

### [249] [ContextNest: Verifiable Context Governance for Autonomous AI Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02116)
*Misha Sulpovar,Benn R. Konsynski,Qaish Kanchwala,Gabe Goodhart*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ContextNext——一个开放规范与参考实现，用于构建受治理的AI可消费知识库。ContextNext在RAG检索层之下提供治理层，通过类型化Markdown文档、集合代数选择器、哈希链版本历史、图级检查点、MCP源节点和审计追踪等机制，确保知识工件的审批、版本、归属和完整性。实验表明，治理方案在过期版本攻击下严格帕累托优于BM25检索（97% vs 93-90%正确率，成本仅1/3），且确定性选择器能实现100%检索确定性（而稠密+HNSW基线在80%查询上非确定性，Jaccard均值仅0.611）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG检索管线只关注相关性，缺乏对知识版本身份、完整性、可追溯性和时间点重构的持久保证，无法应对AI Agent依赖外部知识时的治理需求。

Method: ContextNext规范：1) 类型化Markdown文档+元数据；2) 确定性集合代数选择器；3) contextnest:// URI引用；4) SHA-256哈希链版本历史；5) 图级检查点；6) 通过MCP的源节点；7) Agent上下文消费审计追踪。治理层在检索前确定哪些工件被批准、当前、可归属且完整性已验证。

Result: 实验一（过期版本攻击）：治理选择严格帕累托优于BM25稀疏检索，正确率97% vs 93-90%，输入token成本仅约1/3。实验二（检索确定性）：确定性选择器和BM25在重复查询上Jaccard=1.0；稠密+HNSW基线在80%查询上非确定，平均Jaccard=0.611，最差仅0.210。

Conclusion: 上下文治理能解决检索质量本身无法解决的故障模式（如版本过期、检索非确定性）。ContextNext作为开放规范，为AI Agent提供可审计、可复现的知识消费基础。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents increasingly depend on external knowledge stores, yet most retrieval pipelines provide relevance without durable guarantees of provenance, version identity, integrity, traceability, or point-in-time reconstruction. We formalize this as context governance and present ContextNext, an open specification and reference implementation for governed AI-consumable knowledge vaults. ContextNext does not replace Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG); it supplies the governance layer beneath retrieval, determining which artifacts are approved, current, attributable, and integrity-verified before retrieval systems operate over them.
  The specification combines typed Markdown documents with metadata, deterministic set-algebraic selectors, contextnest:// URI references, SHA-256 hash-chained version histories, graph-level checkpoints, source nodes for live data through the Model Context Protocol (MCP), and audit traces of agent context consumption. These mechanisms let organizations reconstruct which knowledge versions informed an agent output and whether those versions were AI-eligible when consumed.
  We report first empirical results from two controlled experiments. In a stale-version attack isolating the governance-versus-retrieval failure mode, governed selection strictly Pareto-dominates BM25 sparse retrieval, with higher answer-quality pass rate (97% versus 93-90%) at about one-third the input-token cost. In a retrieval-determinism experiment over a 1,060-document corpus, deterministic selectors and BM25 return stable document sets across repeated identical queries (Jaccard 1.0), while a dense+HNSW baseline is non-deterministic on 80% of queries (mean Jaccard 0.611, worst case 0.210). These results suggest that context governance addresses failure modes retrieval quality alone is not designed to resolve. We release a core engine, CLI, and MCP server under open licenses.

Method: Paper-replication 工作流：将每个选定论文声明作为目标并记录证据→代理记录目标→重建论文方法→运行计算实验→链接输出结果与来源及论文声明对比→记录匹配证据在复现报告中的位置→通过验证检查后完成。在四篇科学机器学习论文上进行了十二次独立运行评估。

Abstract: Scientific machine learning papers typically make computational claims, e.g., that the relative mean square error is less than 5% or that the 95% predictive credible interval covers the test data. A coding agent can be prompted to replicate those claims from paper materials alone, but the prompt does not by itself reliably preserve progress or check whether generated evidence supports the paper's claims. We introduce Paper-replication, a workflow that makes each selected paper claim a target with recorded evidence, and implement it as a coding-agent skill. The workflow makes the agent record those targets, reconstruct the paper's method, run computational experiments, link generated outputs to provenance and comparisons with the paper's claims, record where matched evidence appears in the replication report, and pass validation checks before completion. We evaluate Paper-replication on twelve independent runs across four scientific machine learning papers. All twelve workspaces pass the completion gate, and all 158 recorded targets are matched with report coverage. Even in this completed workspace state, repeated runs differ in how papers are divided into targets, in numerical fidelity to the source papers, in elapsed replication time, in the number of intermediate executions replaced before final evidence is accepted, and in the rules used to accept evidence. Paper-replication makes completion depend on workspace evidence and validation checks rather than on the agent's final message.

Abstract: Most LP-from-text benchmarks are static datasets of word problems written and labeled by hand. Once such a dataset is released, its size is fixed, its difficulty is fixed, and every problem can leak into the training data of future LLMs. We present \textbf{A$^{2}$utoLPBench}, a benchmark for testing LLM-driven agents on linear programming problems written in plain text. We first pick a feasible point and dual, then write down a problem for which that point is optimal and the objective value is known. The answer is known by construction, with no solver call and no human annotator. The evaluation environment bundles a reference solver-critic baseline and a Docker image whose usage instructions are written for an LLM-driven agent to read. With these in place, any agent can run the benchmark and get a calibrated score with one command. Because the benchmark is a generator rather than a fixed dataset, it has properties no fixed dataset can match: an unlimited supply of fresh problems, a difficulty knob set by $(n,m)$, ground-truth answers correct by construction, low LLM-side cost per problem relative to human authoring, repeatable scores across independent batches, and resistance to training-data leakage when fresh post-cutoff seed ranges are used.

### [253] [AgenticSTS: A Bounded-Memory Testbed for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02255)
*Xiangchen Cheng,Yunwei Jiang,Jianwen Sun,Zizhen Li,Chuanhao Li,Xiangcheng Cao,Yihao Liu,Fanrui Zhang,Li Jin,Kaipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于类型化检索的有界记忆合约（bounded memory contract）用于长视界LLM智能体，替代传统的追加式无界记忆。在《Slay the Spire 2》游戏中测试，与无记忆基线相比，添加策略技能层后胜率从3/10提升至6/10，但统计上不显著。论文同时发布了包含298条轨迹的可复现测试平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的追加式无界记忆将过去所有观测、工具调用和反思堆叠到每次提示中，导致上下文混杂，难以隔离单个记忆组件的效果。作者希望设计一种有界、可隔离、可消融的记忆合约，以系统化研究记忆组件对长视界决策的影响。

Method: 提出"有界记忆合约"：每次决策从由类型化检索（typed retrieval）组装的全新用户消息出发，不追加原始跨决策记录。在《Slay the Spire 2》中实例化该合约，进行固定-A0消融实验（无记忆基线 vs 添加策略技能层），并跨不同骨干模型进行探测及与公开累积上下文基线对比。

Result: 在固定-A0消融中，无记忆基线胜率3/10，添加策略技能层后胜率6/10（Fisher精确检验p≈0.37，方向性而非统计决定性）。前沿LLM在公开基准上的最低难度胜率为0%，人类开发者报告胜率为16%。发布了298条完整轨迹及配套资源。

Conclusion: 有界记忆合约能够实现对记忆组件的隔离消融，提供了一种可复现、可验证的长视界LLM智能体设计方法论。当前结果仅为操作比较而非合约变量本身的受控检验，未来需更大样本量进行统计验证。

Abstract: Memory for a long-horizon LLM agent is a contract about what each future decision is allowed to see. The simplest contract appends past observations, tool calls, and reflections to every prompt, which makes prior context easy to access but also turns it into a jumbled mixture in which the effect of any single memory component is hard to isolate. We introduce and instrument an alternative bounded contract: every decision is made from a fresh user message assembled by typed retrieval, with no raw cross-decision transcript appended. The prompt thus stays bounded across runs of any length, and any single layer can be ablated in isolation. We instantiate the contract in Slay the Spire 2, a closed-rule stochastic deck-building game whose runs require hundreds of tactical and strategic decisions. A public online benchmark of frontier LLMs on the same game reports zero wins at the lowest difficulty across five configurations, and the developer-reported human win rate at the same difficulty is 16%; the task is hard but not saturated. Within our harness, a fixed-A0 ablation shows the largest observed difference when triggered strategic skills are enabled: the no-store baseline wins 3/10 games and adding the skill layer 6/10. At this sample size the comparison is directional rather than statistically decisive (Fisher exact p\approx0.37); a cross-backbone probe and public accumulating-context baselines are reported as operational comparisons rather than controlled tests of the contract variable itself. We release a reproducible testbed: 298 completed trajectories with condition tags, frozen memory/skill snapshots, prompt records, and analysis scripts -- an agent design and a validated, reusable methodology for studying how explicit memory layers shape long-horizon LLM-agent decisions.

### [254] [A rubric-based controlled comparison of frontier language models on expert-authored clinical reasoning tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02175)
*Samiha A. Ismail,Fan X. Chen,Ali Merali*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个由临床医生编写的小型高难度医学评估数据集，包含5个临床场景和184条加权MECE评分标准。评估三个前沿模型发现：高权重关键标准通过率仅32.4-41.7%，而低权重标准通过率达80-90%，存在临床优先级倒置问题。52%的关键标准无模型通过。LLM自动评分器与专家标签一致性达92.8-94.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有选择题式医学基准已趋饱和，而基于rubric的开放式临床评估（如HealthBench）仍远未解决（其"Hard"子集最高仅32%），亟需更困难、更贴近真实临床推理的评估方法。

Method: 构建5个临床场景（麻醉、内科/家庭医学、急诊医学、产科），每个场景配有从临床医生撰写的金标准答案中提取的原子化、加权、MECE评分标准（每任务25-62条，共184条）。评估GPT 5.4、Claude Opus 4.7、Gemini 3.1 Pro三个前沿模型，使用LLM自动评分器与专家标签对比。

Result: 平均rubric通过率：Claude 0.47、GPT 0.39、Gemini 0.37。权重5关键标准通过率仅32.4-41.7%，权重1标准通过率80-90%。108条关键标准中56条（52%）无模型通过。LLM自动评分器与专家标签一致性92.8-94.7%。

Conclusion: 当前前沿模型存在临床优先级倒置问题（高权重关键标准表现最差），该数据集可作为可扩展的评估管道基础，发展为大规模基准。

Abstract: Multiple-choice medical benchmarks are increasingly saturated, and recent rubric-based evaluations such as HealthBench have shown that open-ended clinical performance is far from solved - its "Hard" subset top score remains 32%. We present a small, deliberately difficult evaluation dataset of five clinician-authored clinical scenarios spanning four specialties (anaesthesia, internal/family medicine, emergency medicine, and obstetrics), each accompanied by an atomic, weighted, MECE rubric (25-62 criteria per task; 184 criteria total) authored from a clinician-drafted golden answer. We evaluate three frontier models: GPT 5.4, Claude Opus 4.7, and Gemini 3.1 Pro. Mean rubric pass rates were 0.47 (Claude), 0.39 (GPT), and 0.37 (Gemini). The central finding is an inversion of clinical priority: the highest-weighted (weight-5, critical) criteria passed at only 32.4-41.7%, while low-stakes weight-1 criteria passed at 80-90%. 56 of 108 critical (weight-5) criteria (52%) were satisfied by no model. Three LLM autoraters reproduced expert met/not-met labels on 92.8-94.7% of 552 graded criteria. We position this as a methods-and-preliminary-findings contribution: the five tasks demonstrate a scalable, defensible pipeline ready to develop into a large-scale benchmark.

### [255] [Automated grading of Linux/bash examinations using large language models: a four-level cognitive taxonomy approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02432)
*Manuel Alonso-Carracedo,Ruben Fernandez-Boullon,Pedro Celard,Francisco J. Rodriguez-Martinez,Lorena Otero-Cerdeira*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了四种前沿大语言模型（GPT、Claude Opus、Gemini、GLM）在命令行考试评分中逼近专家判断的能力。在1200份真实学生答卷上，Gemini 3.0 Pro结合基于评分准则的提示词取得了最高的人机一致性（ICC(3,1)=0.888, MAE=0.10）。研究揭示了题目复杂度是预测LLM评分准确性的可靠指标，并建立了基于认知分类学的人工智能辅助评分框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算教育中命令行考试评分面临可扩展性与可靠性的双重挑战：学生人数增长使人工批改困难，而基于规则的自动评分器无法处理部分正确、等价解法及语法变体等问题，亟需更智能的评分方案。

Method: 采用四级认知分类学（信息检索L1、基本文件操作L2、结构性操作L3、高级系统管理L4），使用两种提示词变体（最小基线与基于评分准则的增强版），对1200份由三位专家独立评分的计算机工程二年级学生真实答卷进行测试。

Result: Gemini 3.0 Pro结合评分准则提示达到最佳性能（ICC(3,1)=0.888, MAE=0.10, Bland-Altman偏差=-0.014）。随分类学等级提升，一致性持续下降。评分准则质量对性能的影响大于模型供应商的选择，结构化提示词持续提升一致性。

Conclusion: 题目复杂度是LLM评分准确性的可靠预测指标；建立了基于分类学的原则性框架，用于判断哪些题目适合AI辅助评分、哪些需要人工复审，同时提供了可迁移的评估协议和提示词模板。

Abstract: Scalable and reliable grading of command-line examinations remains a challenge in computing education, where rising enrolments make manual marking difficult and rule-based autograders cannot handle partial credit, equivalent solutions, or syntactic variation. This paper evaluates whether four frontier Large Language Models (GPT, Claude Opus, Gemini, and GLM) can approximate expert judgment when grading short Linux/bash command responses. The study adopts a four-level cognitive taxonomy that combines cognitive complexity and operational impact, ranging from information retrieval (L1) and basic file manipulation (L2) to structural operations (L3) and advanced system management (L4). The models were tested with two prompt variants, a minimal baseline and a rubric-enhanced version, on 1200 real responses from second-year Computer Engineering students independently graded by three expert instructors. Gemini~3.0 Pro with rubric-guided prompting achieved the highest human-AI agreement (ICC(3,1) = 0.888, MAE = 0.10, Bland-Altman bias = -0.014). Agreement declined consistently as taxonomy level increased, with the largest discrepancies at higher levels. Across all models, rubric quality had a larger effect than provider choice, with structured prompts consistently improving agreement. These results show that question complexity is a reliable predictor of the difficulty LLMs face in grading accurately, and they establish a principled, taxonomy-based framework for determining which questions are suitable for AI-assisted grading and which require human review, while also providing a transferable evaluation protocol and prompt templates.

</details>

*Temitayo Olamilekan Ogunsusi,Lijun Qian,Xishuang Dong*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体软件框架假设中间输出同样可靠，导致早期阶段的错误决策（幻觉）传播至下游智能体，影响最终软件质量。

However, existing approaches typically assume that intermediate agent outputs are equally reliable, leaving them vulnerable to hallucination propagation, where incorrect decisions generated in early development phases are transferred to downstream agents and negatively impact final software quality. To address this challenge, we propose UA-ChatDev, an uncertainty-aware multi-agent software development framework that integrates uncertainty quantification into agent interactions. It introduces a lightweight uncertainty estimation mechanism based on token-level log probabilities to assess the confidence of agent responses and employs phase-aware threshold calibration to selectively trigger retrieval-based verification when uncertainty exceeds acceptable levels. Extensive experiments on the SRDD benchmark demonstrate that UA-ChatDev consistently outperforms existing single-agent and multi-agent software development frameworks across completeness, executability, consistency, and overall quality metrics. We instantiate this setting in EvoPolicyGym, a benchmark built from compact interactive RL environments that evaluates how agents iteratively improve explored policies. On the EvoPolicyGym suite, GPT-5.5 achieves the strongest aggregate rank score and top-two performance on all 16 environments. Beyond leaderboard results, EvoPolicyGym also provides trajectory-level diagnostics that distinguish how agents allocate budget, convert feedback into parametric tuning. These analyses show that strong autonomous policy evolution depends not only on isolated task wins, but on discovering task-appropriate mechanisms and refining policies under bounded feedback.

Abstract: The evolution toward fully autonomous telecommunications networks (Autonomous Network Levels 4-5) requires AI/ML agents to make real-time network decisions without human intervention. However, no standardized runtime mechanism exists to intercept and validate individual inference outputs before they trigger live network state changes, creating risks of erroneous autonomous decisions. This paper proposes the Guard Rail Validation (GRV) framework, a standardizable runtime architecture for intercepting and validating AI-driven decisions before execution. The framework evaluates decisions across multiple weighted dimensions -- including action scope, action type, service criticality, agent autonomy level, reversibility, and temporal behavioural patterns -- to determine a criticality level. Based on this level, graduated validation mechanisms are applied: execute-with-logging, bounds checking, independent agent validation, or multi-agent consensus. The framework additionally provides cross-agent conflict detection with criticality-weighted priority resolution and runtime conformance logging for regulatory compliance (e.g., EU AI Act Article 14). ### [259] [Purified OPSD: On-Policy Self-Distillation Without Losing How to Think](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02234)
*Zhanming Shen,Jintao Tong,Shaotian Yan,Chen Shen,Hao Chen,Wentao Ye,Xiaomeng Hu,Rui Miao,Haobo Wang,Junbo Zhao,Gang Chen,Jieping Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在线自我蒸馏（OPSD）在长思维链推理模型中失败的根本原因——教师监督信号被参考诱导的捷径成分主导，导致学生死记硬背而非学习可迁移的推理能力。作者提出通过构建仅参考教师提取非可迁移成分，并利用点互信息（PMI）构建可蒸馏目标分布，在两个数据集上的四个长CoT模型中验证了该方法优于基线和标准OPSD。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线自我蒸馏（OPSD）在提升LLM推理方面有潜力，但在长思维链（long-CoT）推理模型上始终表现不佳，仅带来边际收益且破坏模型依赖的反思推理能力，亟需探究其失败原因并提出解决方案。

Method: 1) 对教师监督信号进行新颖分解，识别出参考诱导成分（导致死记硬背捷径）和问题条件化、可迁移推理成分；2) 构建仅参考教师（同模型仅以参考为条件，不含问题），隔离非可迁移成分；3) 用点互信息（PMI）将残差信号转化为可蒸馏的PMI目标分布，过滤参考诱导捷径。

Result: 在四个长CoT推理模型、两个数据集上，该方法一致优于基线和标准OPSD，且在整个训练过程中保持了模型自然的认知行为（epistemic behavior）。

Conclusion: OPSD失败的根本原因在于教师监督信号中参考诱导成分主导了学习过程；通过隔离非可迁移成分并利用PMI进行蒸馏，可以有效提升长CoT模型的推理能力，同时避免破坏其反思推理特性。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has emerged as a promising paradigm for improving LLM reasoning, where a privileged teacher with access to reference solutions provides token-level supervision on the student's own generated trajectories. However, we find that OPSD consistently fails on long chain-of-thought (long-CoT) reasoning models, yielding at best marginal gains while destabilizing the reflective reasoning capability these models depend on. Through a novel decomposition of the teacher's supervision signal, we identify the root cause: the teacher's supervision is dominated by a reference-induced component that drives rote memorization of reference-specific shortcuts, while the question-conditioned, inference-transferable component is ignored or actively opposed. Based on this diagnosis, we propose a two-step solution. First, we construct a reference-only teacher (the same model conditioned on the reference without the question) to isolate the non-transferable component of the supervision signal; the residual after subtracting this component captures the question-conditioned, inference-transferable correction. Second, we use pointwise mutual information (PMI) as the mechanism to transform this residual into a well-formed PMI target distribution that the student can directly distill from, filtering out the reference-induced shortcut. Experiments on four long-CoT models across two datasets demonstrate consistent improvements over both the base model and standard OPSD, while preserving the models' natural epistemic behavior throughout training.

</details>

Method: 提出双通道辩论框架，包含公开通道（公开话语进入共享历史）和OTR通道（私下回应记录但不展示给其他参与者）。在10个模型、3个场景、每个场景5个变体下进行实验，通过立场分析、语义相似度、自然语言推理和问卷调查四种聚合分析衡量分歧。

Abstract: LLM agents will increasingly act in socially structured settings where role, audience, and relational context can shape what is advantageous or costly to say. We study whether such social structure, without any explicit objective in the prompt, changes what an agent expresses publicly relative to an off-the-record (OTR) channel elicited under the same condition. We introduce a dual-channel debate framework in which agents produce public utterances that enter the shared history alongside OTR responses that are recorded but never shown to the other participant. Across 10 models, 3 scenarios, and 5 variations within each scenario, alignment-inducing settings produce systematic public-OTR divergence in the targeted agent, with its decision divergence rising from a $\sim$3% baseline to roughly 40%. The effect is consistent across four aggregate analyses: stance, semantic similarity, natural language inference, and survey responses. In some cases, the OTR response explicitly attributes public accommodation to relational pressures, such as career risk or sponsorship obligation. The findings suggest that agent evaluation should extend beyond explicit goals and detect emergent objectives. We present a dual-channel evaluation framework and complementary behavioral measures that operationalize this assessment.

This paper presents Copewell, a novel multi-agent swarm system designed to expand access to mental wellness support through human-centered AI principles. Our architecture introduces three technical innovations: (1) a multi-source assessment framework integrating self-reported, physiological, and contextual data to mitigate algorithmic bias; (2) valence-arousal emotion mapping using Russell's Circumplex Model of Affect to route users to specialized AI agents; and (3) dual-mode intervention delivery combining conversational support with evidence-based sensory wellness protocols. Motivation: LLM在部署时仍可能生成不安全输出，需要在线监控并实时报警。

Method: 采用外部模型的验证器信号，通过阈值化进行报警决策，阈值通过风险控制校准。

Result: 在数学推理和红队测试数据集上，该简单设计与基于序贯假设检验的先进监控器性能相当。

Conclusion: 简单的阈值化实时监控器在LLM安全输出监控中是有效且具有竞争力的方案。

Abstract: Despite alignment training, LLMs remain prone to generating unsafe outputs at deployment time. Monitoring outputs online and raising an alarm when safety can no longer be assumed is therefore critical. We study a simple real-time monitor that turns a verifier signal from an external model into an alarm decision by thresholding, with the threshold calibrated via risk control. In experiments on mathematical reasoning and red teaming datasets, we show that this simple design is competitive with more advanced monitors based on sequential hypothesis testing.

### [263] [A Hippocampus for Linear Attention: An Exact Memory for What the Recurrent State Forgets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02303)
*Wanyun Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HOLA为线性注意力模型引入海马体互补缓存机制，通过保留关键键值对的精确存储（而非强制压缩），在O(1)内存下实现了超越全注意力Transformer++的困惑度，并在长上下文检索任务中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性注意力和状态空间模型将前缀压缩为固定大小循环状态，虽实现O(1)内存但导致有损精确记忆——当键值关联竞争时，早期事实被覆盖，针检索性能下降。

Method: 保留delta-rule状态作为压缩记忆，同时添加有界精确KV缓存形成半参数测试时记忆。缓存写入无需学习淘汰模块，而是保留具有大beta*||e||（实际提交到状态的预测残差）的token；通过解耦的RMSNorm-gamma缓存读取将精确KV对转化为锐利检索而非软平均。

Result: 340M参数在15B SlimPajama上训练，HOLA将Wikitext困惑度从27.32降至22.92（-16.1%），低于全注意力Transformer++（26.88）；LAMBADA困惑度从30.95降至30.26。在线性上下文检索中达到最优，在RULER针检索任务中至32k tokens（16倍训练长度）仍保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 受互补学习系统启发，给线性注意力增加海马体互补机制可有效平衡压缩记忆与精确检索，在保持高效推理的同时提升长上下文事实召回能力。

Abstract: Linear-attention and state-space language models compress the prefix into a fixed-size recurrent state, yielding O(1) memory at the cost of a lossy exact memory: when many key--value associations compete, earlier facts are overwritten and needle recall degrades. Inspired by Complementary Learning Systems, we give linear attention a hippocampal complement. HOLA (Hippocampal Linear Attention) keeps the usual delta-rule state as a compressive memory and adds a bounded exact KV cache, forming a semiparametric test-time memory: the state models linearly compressible structure, while the cache stores associations that should not be forced through that state. The cache writes without a learned eviction module, keeping tokens with large beta * ||e||, the prediction residual actually committed to the state; a decoupled RMSNorm-gamma cache read then turns these exact KV pairs into sharp retrieval rather than soft averaging. At 340M parameters trained on 15B SlimPajama tokens, HOLA lowers Wikitext perplexity from 27.32 to 22.92 (-16.1%), below a full-attention Transformer++ (26.88), and improves LAMBADA perplexity from 30.95 to 30.26. It also achieves the best linear in-context retrieval and remains much more robust than GDN or a matched HOLA+recency cache on RULER needle-in-a-haystack recall out to 32k tokens (16x its training length).

</details>


### [264] [Grounded autonomous research: a fault-tolerant LLM pipeline from corpus to manuscript in frontier computational physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02329)
*Haonan Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个端到端的自主研究代理流水线，从11,083篇凝聚态物理arXiv论文出发，自动完成文献映射、方法校准、第一性原理计算和论文撰写，最终产出包含三项实质性物理发现的出版级手稿。该流水线通过冗余设计（隔离上下文、分布式锚定、对抗性审查）实现容错，并系统量化了文献锚定校准机制的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿物理科学研究与机器学习沙盒环境存在本质差异：物理推理贯穿所有方法选择，工具链文档不完善，校准必须依赖外部文献锚点。现有无框架代理只会引用文献但不会直面其约束，容易从内部先验中幻觉出看似合理但无法验证的结果。因此需要一种能够结构性地强制数值校准的自主研究框架。

Method: 构建了一个六阶段流水线：1) 文献语料库构建（11,083篇近期arXiv论文）；2) 自主构思研究方向（通过映射文献空间）；3) 方法校准（复现已发表文献作为参考锚点）；4) 新颖第一性原理计算；5) 论文撰写（全程基于文献锚定）；6) 容错机制（47次独立上下文会话、2,162次文献咨询事件、仅共享磁盘状态）。设计了两种对照实验：无架构基线（pre-architecture baseline）和无校准消融（no-pilot ablation），以隔离数值校准机制的效果。

Result: 代理自主产出了三项关于交变磁性压电效应的实质性物理发现，并撰写了出版级手稿。容错性来自冗余设计：独立会话隔离、分布式锚定和对抗性审查可捕获单一会话遗漏的错误。前导阶段和后导阶段完全自主，仅在复现失败时需要有限的人工干预（操作知识整理，而非科学方向指导）。两种失效模式对比表明，结构性强制的数值校正是实现文献锚定的关键机制。

Conclusion: 本研究刻画了自主研究代理的基本原语、特征化失效模式和量化的干预模式，为将自主研究扩展到计算物理之外的高风险科学领域奠定了基础。

Abstract: Autonomous-research agents have demonstrated end-to-end LLM automation in machine-learning sandboxes where execution provides calibration. Frontier physical science differs categorically: physical reasoning underlies every methodology choice, toolchains are often underdocumented, and calibration must come from external literature anchors - which unscaffolded agents cite but do not confront, hallucinating plausible, unverifiable results from internal priors. We present a pipeline that runs end-to-end from a corpus of 11,083 recent condensed-matter physics arXiv papers to a publication-grade manuscript with three substantive physics findings (here on altermagnetic piezomagnetism): the agent autonomously conceives a research direction by mapping the corpus, calibrates methodology by reproducing published references, conducts novel first-principles computations, and writes the manuscript - grounded in literature throughout, across 47 fresh-context sessions in six phases sharing only on-disk state, with 2,162 literature-consultation events. Fault tolerance emerges from redundancy: fresh-context isolation, distributed grounding, and adversarial review catch what any single session misses; pre- and post-pilot stages are fully autonomous, and pilot requires bounded human intervention only at reproduction failures - operational knowledge curation, not scientific direction. Two paired failure modes - a pre-architecture baseline and a no-pilot ablation - isolate structurally enforced numerical confrontation at calibration checkpoints as the operative grounding mechanism. The primitives, characterized failure modes, and quantified intervention pattern lay a foundation for autonomous research in high-stakes scientific domains beyond computational physics.

</details>

*Xi Fang,Weijie Xu,Yingqiang Ge,Yuhui Xu,Stephanie Eckman,Chandan K. Reddy*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 个性化LLM通过存储用户属性信息改变输出内容，但现有研究忽略了这种记忆是否会影响模型内部的推理轨迹。在没有真实答案的开放式问题中，需要一种无真值的方法来量化推理漂移。

Method: 提出DRIFTLENS框架，将推理步骤映射到价值类别，比较无记忆轨迹与注入用户属性记忆后的轨迹之间的散度。在4个LLM和10种用户属性上验证，并评估GRPO/DPO后训练对漂移的缓解效果。

Abstract: Personalization changes what a model says to a user; we show that it can also change the reasoning trajectory used to justify the response. Modern LLMs personalize interactions by storing user attributes, preferences, and prior context, then injecting this information into future prompts. We study whether such memory reshapes reasoning on open-ended questions where no single ground-truth answer exists. To quantify this effect, we introduce DRIFTLENS, a ground-truth-free framework that maps each expressed reasoning step to a value category and measures divergence between a question's no-memory trajectory and its trajectory under injected user-attribute memory. We first validate that DRIFTLENS distinguishes content-free pragmatic noise from substantive reasoning changes. Across four LLMs and 10 user-attribute categories, including age, occupation, and disability, user-attribute memory induces medium-to-large reasoning drift above each model's pragmatic-noise floor, even when final answers remain fluent, on-topic, and plausible. We then evaluate GRPO- and DPO-based post-training methods for reducing drift. Both reduce drift, but neither uniformly dominates; effects on downstream capability, helpfulness, and instruction following are model-and reward-dependent. These results suggest that memory-induced reasoning drift is a measurable and only partly mitigated failure mode of personalized language models.

Focus is not on acceleration, but on enforcing temporal synchronization, semantic gating, authorization constraints, and bounded coordination behavior directly in hardware. Semantic reasoning remains adaptive and software-driven, while embedded coordination semantics become deterministic.

### [270] [G-RRM: Guiding Symbolic Solvers with Recurrent Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02491)
*Timo Bertram,Sidhant Bhavnani,Richard Freinschlag,Erich Kobler,Andreas Mayr,Günter Klambauer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出G-RRM方法，将符号等变循环推理模型（SE-RRM）与经典符号求解器（回溯法、Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0）结合，用于约束满足问题。实验表明，神经引导的加速效果取决于两个条件：问题组合搜索空间足够大，且求解器架构能动态覆写分支选择。满足条件时，回溯法加速33.3倍，Glucose 4.1加速1.70倍；而CaDiCaL因尊重注入提示而无法覆写，未见显著加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索神经引导（SE-RRM）是否能以及何时能提升符号求解器（回溯法、SAT求解器）在约束满足问题上的搜索效率。

Method: 提出G-RRM框架：SE-RRM作为神经求解器生成完整解方案，引导经典符号求解器（回溯法、Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0）进行搜索；通过设计实验系统考察求解器架构对神经提示的响应机制（能否动态覆写分支选择）以及问题组合空间规模对加速效果的影响。

Result: 在9×9数独上，SE-RRM正确率91.1%时，回溯法加速33.3倍，Glucose 4.1加速1.70倍；25×25完美提示下Glucose 4.1保持1.17倍加速。CaDiCaL 3.0无显著加速（中位数1.02倍），甚至出现显著平均减速（0.90倍）。加速关键条件：问题需有广阔组合搜索空间，且求解器能动态覆写神经提示。

Conclusion: 神经引导对符号求解器的加速效果高度依赖于求解器架构（能否动态修正分支选择）和问题本身的组合搜索规模；CaDiCaL因固守注入提示而无法受益，阐明了神经-符号融合方法有效性的边界条件。

Abstract: In this work, we focus on SE-RRMs, a symbol-equivariant instantiation of RRMs that exhibits improved extrapolation to larger problem sizes. We propose a neuro-symbolic approach, ``Guiding with Recurrent Reasoning Models'' (G-RRM), which integrates SE-RRMs with symbolic solvers for constraint satisfaction problems. SE-RRMs act as neural solvers that generate full solution proposals and guide classical symbolic solvers, such as backtracking or SAT-based methods like Glucose 4.1 and CaDiCaL 3.0.0, that produce globally correct solutions. Centrally, we investigate when neural guidance with G-RRM improves the search efficiency of symbolic solvers. %
Our experiments show that the efficacy of G-RRM depends on two conditions: first, the problem instances must have an expansive combinatorial search space to expose potential gains, and second, the solver architecture must be capable of dynamically overwriting its branching choices to recover when neural hints are imperfect. When these conditions hold, guidance drives median conflict counts to zero and yields significant wall-clock speedups: on $9\times9$ Sudoku, where the SE-RRM correctly solves $91.1\%$ of instances, backtracking accelerates by $33.3\times$ and Glucose 4.1 by $1.70\times$ (median, $p<0.001$), with Glucose 4.1 retaining a $1.17\times$ speedup on perfect-hint $25\times25$ grids. In contrast, CaDiCaL 3.0.0, whose runtime is overhead-dominated and which always respects the injected branching hints rather than overwriting them, shows no significant speedup (median $1.02\times$, n.s.) and even a small significant mean slowdown ($0.90\times$) on $9\times9$. These results delineate the regimes in which neural guidance translates into practical speedups.
